### Post by skippylou on 2015-11-17
I have been using 14.04LTS and a Samsung ML1630 which stopped working today.  I went to "System Settings" and looked for the "Printers" icon.  IT'S GONE!  Am I looking in the wrong place or is something strange going on?

PS  It may be coincidental but I installed several packages yesterday:  Emacs, SBCL (Steel Bank Common Lisp), Slime and a few other packages to get some missing header files.  The icon for Ubuntu Software Center also disappeared and Google Chrome no longer functions.
